Question #1 (ID: 706247)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=p^{2}-3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{\frac{-2}{3}}+2[/math] এবং [math]f(x)=\ln (1+x) ; x \geq 0.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math](25)^{x}=(125)^{y}[/math] হলে [math]x: y[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]A=0[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]3 p^{3}+9 p=8[/math]
গ. [math]f(x)[/math] এর বর্ণনাসহ লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math](25)^{x}=(125)^{y}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left(5^{2}\right)^{x}=\left(5^{3}\right)^{y} \text{ বা, } 5^{2 x}=5^{3 y} \Rightarrow 2 x=3 y \Rightarrow \frac{x}{y}=\frac{3}{2}\\\therefore \quad x: y=3: 2 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=p^{2}-3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{\frac{-2}{3}}+2[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]A=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow p^{2}-3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{\frac{-2}{3}}+2=0 \text{ বा, } p^{2}=3^{\frac{2}{3}}-2+3^{\frac{-2}{3}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{2}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 3^{\frac{-1}{3}}+\left(3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2}\\\Rightarrow p^{2}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2}\\\Rightarrow p=3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow p^{3}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{3}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right) \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{3}=3-3^{-1}-3 \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}-\frac{1}{3}} \cdot \mathrm{p}\left[\because 3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}=p\right] \\\Rightarrow p^{3}=3-\frac{1}{3}-3 \cdot 3^{0} \cdot p \\\Rightarrow p^{3}=3-\frac{1}{3}-3 p \cdot\left[\because 3^{0}=1\right] \\\Rightarrow p^{3}=\frac{9-1-9 p}{3} \\\Rightarrow 3 p^{3}=8-9 p\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad 3 p^{3}+9 p=8[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\ln (1+x) ; x \geq 0[/math]
x এর কয়েকটি মান নিয়ে y এর মান নিম্নের ছকে দেখানো হলো:[math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|c|r|r|}\hline \mathrm{x} & 0 & 3 & 5 & 8 & 11 \\\hline \mathrm{y} & 0 & 1.386 & 1.792 & 2.197 & 2.485 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
এখন, ছক কাগজে x-অক্ষ XOX' এবং y-অক্ষ YOY' আঁকি। উভয় অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম বর্গের প্রতি বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য 1 একক ধরে ছকে প্রাপ্ত বিন্দুগুলো স্থাপন করে যোগ করি। তাহলে প্রাপ্ত বক্ররেখাই [math]y=f(x)=\ln (1+x)[/math]
 লেখ।
[Image]

Question #2 (ID: 706248)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt[x]{a}=\sqrt[y]{b}=\sqrt[z]{c}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{a}=\mathrm{c}[/math] হলে দেখো যে, [math]\mathrm{x}=\mathrm{z}.[/math]
খ. [math]\mathrm{x=\frac{1}{2}, y=\frac{1}{3}}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\left(\frac{a}{b}\right)^{\frac{3}{2}}+\left(\frac{b}{a}\right)^{\frac{2}{3}}=a^{\frac{1}{2}}+b^{-\frac{1}{3}}.[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm{a b c=1}[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{\frac{1}{p^{-x}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{1}{p^{-y}+p^{z}+1}+\frac{1}{p^{-z}+p^{x}+1}=1}.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sqrt[x]{a}=\sqrt[y]{b}=\sqrt[z]{c}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sqrt[x]{a}=\sqrt[2]{c} \Rightarrow a^{\frac{1}{x}}=c^{\frac{1}{z}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow c^{\frac{1}{x}}=c^{\frac{1}{z}}[\because a=c]\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{x}=\frac{1}{z}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x=z[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\sqrt[x]{a}=\sqrt[y]{b}=\sqrt[2]{c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt[x]{a}=\sqrt[z]{b}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a^{\frac{1}{x}}=b^{\frac{1}{y}}[/math]
 [math]x=\frac{1}{2}, y=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
 হলে আমরা পাই, [math]a^{2}=b^{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore a=b^{\frac{3}{2}}[/math]
আবার, [math]a^{2}=b^{3} \Rightarrow b^{3}=a^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore b=a^{\frac{2}{3}}[/math]
এখন, বামপক্ষ [math]=\left(\frac{a}{b}\right)^{\frac{3}{2}}+\left(\frac{b}{a}\right)^{\frac{2}{3}}=\frac{a^{3 / 2}}{b^{3 / 2}}+\frac{b^{2 / 3}}{a^{2 / 3}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{a^{3 / 2}}{a}+\frac{b^{2 / 3}}{b} \quad\left[\because a=b^{3 / 2}, \mathrm{~b}=\mathrm{a}^{2 / 3}\right] \\=a^{\frac{3}{2}-1}+b^{\frac{2}{3}-1} \\=a^{\frac{1}{2}}+\mathrm{b}^{-\frac{1}{3}} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore\left(\frac{a}{b}\right)^{\frac{3}{2}}+\left(\frac{b}{a}\right)^{\frac{2}{3}}=a^{\frac{1}{2}}+b^{-\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\sqrt[x]{a}=\sqrt[y]{b}=\sqrt[z]{c}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \sqrt[y]{a}=\sqrt[y]{b}[/math]
 এবং [math]\sqrt[y]{b}=\sqrt[z]{c}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a^{\frac{1}{x}}=b^{\frac{1}{y}} \quad \Rightarrow b^{\frac{1}{y}}=c^{\frac{1}{z}} \\\Rightarrow a=b^{\frac{x}{y}} \quad \therefore b=c^{\frac{y}{2}} \\\Rightarrow a=\left(\frac{y}{c^{z}}\right)^{\frac{x}{y}} \\\therefore \quad a=c^{\frac{x}{z}}\end{array}[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]a b c=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}c^{\frac{x}{2}} \cdot c^{z} \cdot c=1 \\\Rightarrow c^{\frac{x}{z}+\frac{y}{z}+1}=c^{0} \quad \Rightarrow \frac{x}{z}+\frac{y}{z}+1=0 \\\Rightarrow \frac{x+y+z}{z}=0 \quad \Rightarrow x+y+z=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad y+z=-x[/math]
 এবং [math]x+z=-y^{2}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1}{p^{-x}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{1}{p^{-y}+p^{2}+1}+\frac{1}{p^{-2}+p^{x}+1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{p^{-x}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{1}{\frac{1}{p^{y}}+p^{z}+1}+\frac{1}{\frac{1}{p^{z}}+p^{x}+1} \\=\frac{1}{p^{-x}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{p^{y}}{1+p^{y} \cdot p^{z}+p^{y}}+\frac{p^{z}}{1+p^{x} \cdot p^{z}+p^{z}} \\=\frac{1}{p^{y+z}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{p^{y}}{1+p^{y+z}+p^{y}}+\frac{p^{z}}{1+p^{x+z}+p^{z}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{p^{y+z}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{p^{y}}{1+p^{y+z}+p^{y}}+\frac{p^{2}}{1+p^{-y}+p^{z}}[\because x+z=-y] \\=\frac{1}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}+\frac{p^{y}}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}+\frac{p^{z}}{1+\frac{1}{p^{y}}+p^{z}} \\=\frac{1}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}+\frac{p^{y}}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}+\frac{p^{y} \cdot p^{z}}{p^{y}+1+p^{y} \cdot p^{z}} \\=\frac{1}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}+\frac{p^{y}}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}+\frac{p^{y+z}}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}{1+p^{y}+p^{y+z}}=1=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1}{p^{-x}+p^{y}+1}+\frac{1}{p^{-y}+p^{z}+1}+\frac{1}{p^{-z}+p^{x}+1}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #3 (ID: 706249)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a=x y^{p-1}, b=x y^{q-1}, c=x y^{r-1}[/math] এবং [math]f(x)=\ln \frac{4+x}{4-x}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math](16)^{2 x}=4^{x+1}[/math] হলে, [math]x=[/math] কত?
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](q-r) \log _{k} a+(r-p) \log _{k} b+(p-q) \log _{k} c=0.[/math]
গ. [math]f(x)=\ln \frac{4+x}{4-x}[/math] ফাংশনের ডোমেন ও রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math](16)^{2 x}=4^{x+1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left(4^{2}\right)^{2 x}=4^{x+1}\\\Rightarrow 4^{4 x}=4^{x+1} \text{.}\\\Rightarrow 4 x=x+1\\\Rightarrow 3 x=1\\\therefore \quad x=\frac{1}{3} \text{ (Ans.)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a=x y^{p-1}, b=x y^{q-1}, c=x y^{r-1}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=(q-r) \log _{k} a+(r-p) \log _{k} b+(p-q) \log _{k} c[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\log _{k} a^{q-r}+\log _{k} b^{r-p}+\log _{k} c^{p-q} \\=\log _{k}\left(x y^{p-1}\right)^{q-r}+\log _{k}\left(x y^{q-1}\right)^{r-p}+\log _{k}\left(x y^{r-1}\right)^{p-q} \\=\log _{k} x^{q-r}+\log _{k} y^{(p-1)(q-r)}+\log _{k} x^{r-p}+\log _{k} y^{(q-1)(r-p)} \\\quad+\log _{k} x^{p-q}+\log _{k} y^{(r-1)(p-q)} \\=\log _{k}\left(x^{q-r} \cdot x^{r-p} \cdot x^{p-q}\right)+\log _{k}\left\{y^{(p-1)(q-r)} \cdot y^{(q-1)(r-p)} \left.y^{(r-1)(p-q)}\right\}\right. \\=\log _{k}\left(x^{q-r+r-p+p-q}\right)+\log _{k}\left(y^{p q-p r-q+r+q r-p q-r+p+p r-q r-p+q}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\log _{k} x^{0}+\log _{k} y^{0}=\log _{k} 1+\log _{k} 1=0=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore(q-r) \log _{k} a+(r-p) \log _{k} b+(p-q) \log _{k} c=0[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\ln \frac{4+x}{4-x}[/math]
যেহেতু লগারিদম শুধুমাত্র ধনাত্মক বাস্তব সংখ্যার জন্য সংজ্ঞায়িত হয়, সেহেতু [math]\frac{4+x}{4-x}>0[/math]
 যদি [math]\text { (i) } 4+x>0[/math]
 এবং [math]4-x>0[/math]
 হয়অথবা [math]\text { (ii) } 4+x-4[/math]
 [math]-x>-4[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]=\{x:-4[math]\begin{array}{l}=(-4, \infty) \cap(-\infty, 4) \\=(-4,4)\end{array}[/math]
শর্ত (ii) হতে পাই, [math]x4[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]=\{x: x4\}=\varnothing[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত ফাংশনের ডোমেন[math]\mathrm{D}_{f}=[/math]
 শর্ত (i) ও (ii) এ প্রাপ্ত ডোমেনের সংযোগ[math]\begin{array}{l}=(-4,4) \cup \varnothing \\=(-4,4)\end{array}[/math]
রেঞ্জঃ [math]y=f(x)=\ln \frac{4+x}{4-x}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow e^{y}=\frac{4+x}{4-x}\\\Rightarrow 4+x=4 e^{y}-x e^{y}\\\Rightarrow x+x e^{y}=4 e^{y}-4\\\Rightarrow x\left(1+e^{y}\right)=4\left(e^{y}-1\right)\\\Rightarrow x=\frac{4\left(e^{y}-1\right)}{e^{y}+1}\end{array}[/math]
y এর সকল বাস্তব মানের জন্য x এর মান বাস্তব হয়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত ফাংশনের রেঞ্জ [math]R_{f}=\mathbb{R}[/math]
 [math]\text { Ans. }[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]D_{f}=(-4,4)[/math]
 এবং রেঞ্জ [math]\mathrm{R}_{f}=\mathbb{R}[/math]

Question #10 (ID: 706256)

Question:
[math]\mathrm{A}=\ln \frac{7-x}{7+x}, B=\frac{x(y+z-x)}{\log _{k} x}=\frac{y(z+x-y)}{\log _{k} y}=\frac{z(x+y-z)}{\log _{k} z}[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]x^{\log _{a} y}=y^{\log _{a} x}[/math]
খ. [math]A[/math] এর ডোমেন ও রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]B[/math] হতে দেখাও যে, [math]x^{y} y^{x}=y^{z} z^{y}=z^{x} x^{z}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:

Question #13 (ID: 706236)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=3^{2 x+2}[/math] এবং [math]g(x)=27^{x+1}[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math](\sqrt{a}-\sqrt{b})(a+\sqrt{a b}+b)=a^{\frac{3}{2}}-b^{\frac{3}{2}}[/math]
খ. [math]3 f(x)+3 g(x)=108[/math] হলে x এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]h(x)=\frac{g(x)}{f(x)}[/math] হলে h(x) এর লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন করে ডোমেন ও রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math](\sqrt{a}-\sqrt{b})(a+\sqrt{a b}+b)[/math]
 [math]=(\sqrt{a}-\sqrt{b})\left\{(\sqrt{a})^{2}+\sqrt{a} \cdot \sqrt{b}+(\sqrt{b})^{2}\right\}[/math]
 [math]=(\sqrt{a})^{3}-(\sqrt{b})^{3}=\left(a^{\frac{1}{2}}\right)^{3}-\left(b^{\frac{1}{2}}\right)^{3}=a^{\frac{3}{2}}-b^{\frac{3}{2}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=3^{2 x+2}[/math]
 [math]g(x)=27^{x+1}[/math]
এবং [math]3 f(x)+3 g(x)=108[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow f(x)+g(x)=36\\\Rightarrow 3^{2 x+2}+27^{x+1}=36\\\Rightarrow 3^{2 x+2}+3^{3 x+3}=36\\\Rightarrow 3^{2 x} \cdot 9+3^{3 x} \cdot 27=36\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3^{2 x}+3^{3 x} \cdot 3=4[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে 9 দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3^{3 x} \cdot 3+3^{2 x}-4=0 \\\Rightarrow 3\left(3^{x}\right)^{3}+\left(3^{x}\right)^{2}-4=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 a^{3}+a^{2}-4=0[/math]
 [ধরি, [math]3^{x}=a[/math]
][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3 a^{3}-3 a^{2}+4 a^{2}-4=0 \\\Rightarrow 3 a^{2}(a-1)+4\left(a^{2}-1\right)=0 \\\Rightarrow 3 a^{2}(a-1)+4(a+1)(a-1)=0 \\\therefore(a-1)\left(3 a^{2}+4 a+4\right)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]a-1=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a=1\\\Rightarrow 3^{x}=3^{0}\end{array}[/math]
অথবা, [math]3 a^{2}+4 a+4=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a=\frac{-4 \pm \sqrt{16-48}}{6}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-4 \pm \sqrt{-32}}{6}[/math]
 যা গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়।[math]\therefore \mathbf{x}=0 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}g(x)=27^{x+1}=3^{3 x+3} \\f(x)=3^{2 x+2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore h(x)=\frac{g(x)}{f(x)}=\frac{3^{3 x+3}}{3^{2 x+2}}=3^{3 x+3-2 x-2}=3^{x+1}[/math]
ধরি, [math]y=h(x)=3^{x+1}[/math]
x এর কয়েকটি মানের জন্য y এর মান নির্ণয় করে প্রদত্ত সমীকরণের লেখের কয়েকটি বিন্দুর স্থানাঙ্ক নির্ণয় করি:[math]\begin{array}{|r|r|r|r|c|}\hline \mathrm{x} & 0 & -1 & 0.5 & -2 \\\hline \mathrm{y} & 3 & 1 & 5.2 & 0.33 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]
সারণি হতে প্রাপ্ত বিন্দুগুলো ছক কাগজে স্থাপন করে সমীকরণটির লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন করি। উভয় অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম 5 বর্গ ঘর = 1 একক ধরা হল।
[Image]
লেখ হতে দেখা যায় যে, x এর সকল বাস্তব মানের জন্য y এর ধনাত্মক বাস্তব মান পাওয়া যায়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোম, [math]h=\mathbb{R}[/math]
 এবং রেঞ্জ, [math]h=(0, \infty) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #14 (ID: 706237)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \mathrm{m}^{2}=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{-\frac{2}{3}}-2 ; \mathrm{m} \geq 0[/math] [math]\text { (ii) } A=\frac{x y+z x-x^{2}}{\log _{k} x}, B=\frac{y z+x y-y^{2}}{\log _{k} y}[/math] এবং [math]C=\frac{z x+y z-z}{\log _{k} z}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\log _{\sqrt{a}} b \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} c \times \log _{\sqrt{c}} d+\log _{\sqrt{d}}^{a}=16[/math] প্রমাণ কর।
খ. (i) হতে দেখাও যে, [math]5 m^{3}+15 m-24=0.[/math]
গ. (ii) হতে A = B = C হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^{y} y^{x}=y^{z} z^{y}=z^{x} x^{z}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ [math]=\log _{\sqrt{a}} \mathrm{~b} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} \mathrm{c} \times \log _{\sqrt{c}} \mathrm{~d} \times \log _{\sqrt{d}} a[/math]
 [math]=\log _{\sqrt{a}}(\sqrt{b})^{2} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}}(\sqrt{c})^{2} \times \log _{\sqrt{c}}(\sqrt{d})^{2} \times \log _{\sqrt{d}}(\sqrt{a})^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2 \log _{\sqrt{a}} \sqrt{b} \times 2 \log _{\sqrt{b}} \sqrt{c} \times 2 \cdot \log _{\sqrt{c}} \sqrt{d} \times 2 \log _{\sqrt{d}} \sqrt{a} \\=16 \log _{\sqrt{a}} \sqrt{b} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} \sqrt{c} \times \log _{\sqrt{c}} \sqrt{d} \times \log _{\sqrt{d}} \sqrt{a} \\=16 \log _{\sqrt{a}} \sqrt{b} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} \sqrt{c} \times \log _{\sqrt{c}} \sqrt{a}\left[\because \log _{a} \mathrm{P}=\log _{a} b \times \log _{b} p\right] \\=16 \log _{\sqrt{a}} \sqrt{b} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} \sqrt{a}=16 \cdot \log _{\sqrt{a}} \sqrt{a}=16.1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=16=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \log _{\sqrt{\mathrm{a}}} \mathrm{b} \times \log _{\sqrt{b}} \mathrm{c} \times \log _{\sqrt{c}} \mathrm{~d} \times \log _{\sqrt{\mathrm{d}}} \mathrm{a}=16[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]m^{2}=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{-\frac{2}{3}}-2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{2}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}-2: 5^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 5^{\frac{-1}{3}}+\left(5^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2} \Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{2}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow m=5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}[/math]
 [বর্গমূল করে] [math]\ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [ঘন করে][math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(5^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3.5^{\frac{1}{3}} .5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=5-5^{-1}-3.5^{0} \mathrm{~m}[/math]
 [(i) থেকে মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=5-\frac{1}{5}-3 \mathrm{~m} \quad \Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=\frac{25-1-15 \mathrm{~m}}{5} \\\Rightarrow 5 \mathrm{~m}^{3}=24-15 \mathrm{~m}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 5 m^{3}+15 m-24=0[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\frac{x y+z x-x^{2}}{\log _{k} x}=\frac{x(y+z-x)}{\log _{k} x}[/math]
 [math]B=\frac{y z+x y-y^{2}}{\log _{k} y}=\frac{y(z+x-y)}{\log _{k} y}[/math]
 [math]C=\frac{z x+y z-z^{2}}{\log _{k} z}=\frac{z(x+y-z)}{\log _{k} z}[/math]
 এবং [math]A=B=C[/math]
ধরি, [math]\frac{x(y+z-x)}{\log _{k} x}=\frac{y(z+x-y)}{\log _{k} y}=\frac{z(x+y-z)}{\log _{k} z}=m[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} x=\frac{x(y+z-x)}{m}[/math]
আবার, [math]\log _{k} y=\frac{y(z+x-y)}{m}[/math]
 এবং [math]\log _{k} z=\frac{z(x+y-z)}{m}[/math]
এখন,[math]\begin{aligned}y \log _{k} x+x \log _{k} y & =\frac{x y(y+z-x)}{m}+\frac{x y(z+x-y)}{m} \\& =\frac{x y}{m}(y+z-x+z+x-y)=\frac{2 x y z}{m}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \log _{k} x^{y}+\log _{k} y^{x}=\frac{2 x y z}{m}\left[\because \log _{k} p^{r}=r \log _{k} p\right]\\\Rightarrow \log _{k} x^{y} y^{x}=\frac{2 x y z}{m} \therefore x^{y} y^{x}=k^{\frac{2 x y z}{m}}\ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }\end{array}[/math]
আবার, [math]z \log _{k} y+y \log _{k} z=\frac{y z(z+x-y)}{m}+\frac{y z(x+y-z)}{m}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \log _{k} y^{z}+\log _{k} z^{y}=\frac{y z}{m}(z+x-y+x+y-z) \\\Rightarrow \log _{k} y^{z} z^{y}=\frac{2 x y z}{m} \therefore y^{z} z^{y}=k^{\frac{2 x y z}{m}} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }\end{array}[/math]
পুনরায়, [math]x \log _{k} z+z \log _{k} x=\frac{z x(x+y-z)}{m}+\frac{z x(y+z-x)}{m}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \log _{k} z^{x}+\log _{k} x^{z}=\frac{z x}{m}(x+y-z+y+z-x)\\\Rightarrow \log _{k} z^{x} x^{z}=\frac{2 x y z}{\dot{m}} \therefore z^{x} x^{z}=k^{\frac{2 x y z}{m}} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (iii) } \end{array}[/math]
সুতরাং (i), (ii) ও (iii) নং থেকে পাই,[math]x^{y} y^{x}=y^{z} z^{y}=z^{x} x^{z}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:

Question #15 (ID: 706238)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=1+\log _{x} y z, B=2+\log _{y} z x, C=3+\log _{z} x y[/math] এবং [math]a^{2}+2=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]

Options:
ক. B = 4 হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{x}{y}=\frac{y}{z}[/math]
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]5 a^{3}+15 a-24=0[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]A^{-1}+(B-1)^{-1}+(C-2)^{-1}=1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=2+\log _{y} z x[/math]
 [math]B=4[/math]
 হলে, [math]2+\log _{y} z x=4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{y} x z=2 \Rightarrow y^{2}=x z[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{y}{x}=\frac{z}{y}[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে xy দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\therefore \frac{x}{y}=\frac{y}{z}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খসৃজনশীল ২৬(খ) নং প্রশ্নের সমাধান দ্রষ্টব্য। পৃষ্ঠা-২১১ [math]\\[/math]
 গসৃজনশীল ৩(খ) নং প্রশ্নের সমাধান দ্রষ্টব্য। পৃষ্ঠা-২০৩

Question #16 (ID: 706239)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p=\log _{5}\left(24+\sqrt{x^{2}-14 x+50}\right)[/math] এবং [math]q=2+3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\log _{k}\left(\frac{x^{\mathrm{m}}}{\mathrm{y}^{\mathrm{m}}}\right)+\log _{\mathrm{k}}\left(\frac{y^{\mathrm{m}}}{\mathrm{z}^{\mathrm{m}}}\right)+\log _{\mathrm{k}}\left(\frac{\mathrm{z}^{\mathrm{m}}}{\mathrm{x}^{\mathrm{m}}}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]q^{3}-6 q^{2}+3 q-2=0[/math]
গ. [math]p = 2[/math] হলে [math]x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l} \log _{k}\left(\frac{x^{m}}{y^{m}}\right)+\log _{k}\left(\frac{y^{m}}{z^{m}}\right)+\log _{k}\left(\frac{z^{m}}{x^{m}}\right) \\=\log _{k}\left(\frac{x^{m}}{y^{m}} \cdot \frac{y^{m}}{z^{m}} \cdot \frac{z^{m}}{x^{m}}\right)[\because \log (x y)=\log x+\log y] \\=\log _{k} 1=0[\because \log 1=0]=0 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]q=2+3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow q-2=3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}} \Rightarrow (q-2)^{3}=\left(3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [ঘন করে][math]\Rightarrow q^{3}-3 \cdot q^{2} \cdot 2+3 \cdot q \cdot 4-8=3^{2}+3+3 \cdot 3^{\frac{2}{3}} \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}}\left(3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left[\because(x+y)^{3}=x^{3}+y^{3}+3 x y(x+y)\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow q^{3}-6 q^{2}+12 q-8=9+3+3.3(q-2)\left[\because q-2=3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right] \\\Rightarrow q^{3}-6 q^{2}+12 q-8=12+9(q-2) \\\Rightarrow q^{3}-6 q^{2}+12 q-8=12+9 q-18 \\\Rightarrow q^{3}-6 q^{2}+12 q-8=9 q-6 \\\Rightarrow q^{3}-6 q^{2}+12 q-8-9 q+6=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore q^{3}-6 q^{2}+3 q-2=0[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]p=\log _{5}\left(24+\sqrt{x^{2}-14 x+50}\right)[/math]
 এবং [math]p=2[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \log _{5}\left(24+\sqrt{\mathrm{x}^{2}-14 \mathrm{x}}+50\right)=2 \\\Rightarrow 24+\sqrt{\mathrm{x}^{2}-14 \mathrm{x}+50}=5^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{x^{2}-14 x+50}=25-24 \Rightarrow x^{2}-14 x+50=(1)^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x^{2}-14 x+50=1 \Rightarrow x^{2}-14 x+49=0 \\\Rightarrow x^{2}-2 . x .7+7^{2}=0 \Rightarrow (x-7)^{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow x-7=0 \quad \therefore x=7 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #17 (ID: 706240)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{x^{p}}=\frac{1}{y q}=\frac{1}{z^{r}},m=2, n=3[/math] এবং [math]g^{2}=h^{3}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]3+7 x-5 x^{2}=0[/math] সমীকরণটির মূলদ্বয়ের প্রকৃতি নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\left(\frac{h}{g}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{n}}{\mathrm{m}}}+\left(\frac{\mathrm{h}}{\mathrm{g}}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{n}}}=\sqrt{\mathrm{g}}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{\mathrm{h}}}[/math]
গ. [math]x y z=1[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{a^{q}+a^{-r}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{r}+a^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{p}+a^{-q}+1}=1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]3+7 x-5 x^{2}=0[/math]
 অর্থাৎ, [math]-5 x^{2}+7 x+3=0[/math]
সমীকরণটিকে [math]a x^{2}+b x+c=0[/math]
সমীকরণের সাথে তুলনা করে পাই,[math]a=-5, b=7, c=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নিশ্চায়ক [math]=b^{2}-4 a c=7^{2}-4(-5) \cdot 3=49+60[/math]
 [math]=109>0[/math]
 কিন্তু পূর্ণ বর্গ নয়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত সমীকরণের মূলদ্বয় বাস্তব, অসমান ও অমূলদ হবে। [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{m}=2 \\\mathrm{n}=3\end{array}[/math]
এখন,বামপক্ষ [math]=\left(\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{g} \\\mathrm{h}\end{array}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{n}}{\mathrm{m}}}+\left(\frac{\mathrm{h}}{\mathrm{g}}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{n}}}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{\mathrm{g}}{\mathrm{h}}\right)^{\frac{3}{2}}+\left(\frac{\mathrm{h}}{\mathrm{g}}\right)^{\frac{2}{3}}[/math]
 [m ও n এর মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}=\left(\frac{\mathrm{g}^{3}}{\mathrm{~h}^{3}}\right)^{\frac{1}{2}}+\left(\frac{h^{2}}{\mathrm{~g}^{2}}\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}=\left(\frac{\mathrm{g}^{3}}{\mathrm{~g}^{\frac{1}{2}}}\right)^{2}+\left(\frac{\mathrm{h}^{2}}{\mathrm{~h}^{3}}\right)^{\frac{1}{3}} \\=\mathrm{g}^{\frac{1}{2}}+\left(\mathrm{h}^{-1}\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}=\sqrt{g}+h^{-\frac{1}{3}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{g}+\left(h^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{-1}=\sqrt{g}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{h}}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore\left(\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{g} \\\mathrm{h}\end{array}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{n}}{\mathrm{m}}}+\left(\frac{\mathrm{h}}{\mathrm{g}}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{n}}}=\sqrt{\mathrm{g}}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{h}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[বি.দ্র: প্রশ্নে ভুল আছে, বামপক্ষে [math]\left(\frac{\mathrm{h}}{\mathrm{g}}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{n}}{\mathrm{m}}}[/math]
 এর স্থলে [math]\left(\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{g} \\\mathrm{h}\end{array}\right)^{\frac{\mathrm{n}}{\mathrm{m}}}[/math]
 হবে] [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\frac{1}{x^p}=\frac{1}{y^q}=\frac{1}{z^r}=[/math]
ধরি, [math]\frac{1}{x^p}=\frac{1}{y^q}=\frac{1}{z^r}=k[/math]
তাহলে, [math]\frac{1}{x^p}=k[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x=\mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{p}}[/math]
একইভাবে, [math]y=k^{q}, z=k^{r}[/math]
আবার, [math]x y z=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore k^{p} \cdot k^{q} \cdot k^{r}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow k^{p+q+r}=k^{0}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r}=0[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1}{a^{q}+a^{-r}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{r}+a^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{p}+a^{-q}+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{a^{q}+\frac{1}{a^{r}}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{r}+a^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{p}+a^{-q}+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{a^{p}+\frac{1}{a^{q}}+1}[/math]
 [math][\because \mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r}=0 \therefore \mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r}=-\mathrm{p}][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{a^{r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{a^{q}}{a^{p+q}+a^{q}+1} \\=\frac{a^{r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{a^{q}}{a^{-r}+a^{q}+1} \\=\frac{a^{r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{a^{q}}{\frac{1}{a^{r}}+a^{q}+1} \\=\frac{a^{r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}+\frac{a^{q} \cdot a^{r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{r}+1+a^{q+r}}{1+a^{r}+a^{q+r}}=1=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1}{a^{q}+a^{-r}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{r}+a^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{p}+a^{-q}+1}=1[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #18 (ID: 706241)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\frac{1}{y^{q}+y^{-r}+1}+\frac{1}{y^{r}+y^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{y^{p}+y^{-q}+1}[/math] এবং [math]\log _{e}(3+x)=2 \log _{e} x.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\log \sqrt{27} \mathrm{~m}=3 \frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে, [math]\mathrm {m}[/math]-এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]p+q+r=0[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]A=1.[/math]
গ. ২য় সমীকরণ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x=\frac{\sqrt{13}+1}{2}.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\log \sqrt{27} m=3 \frac{1}{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \log _{27} m=\frac{10}{3} \\\Rightarrow m=(\sqrt{27})^{\frac{10}{3}}=\left(3^{\frac{3}{2}}\right)^{\frac{10}{3}}=3^{5}=243 \\\therefore \quad m=243 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}A=\frac{1}{y^{q}+y^{-r}+1}+\frac{1}{y^{r}+y^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{y^{p}+y^{-q}+1} \\=\frac{1}{y^{q}+\frac{1}{y^{r}}+1}+\frac{1}{y^{r}+y^{-p}+1}+\frac{1}{y^{p}+y^{-q}+1}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{y^{r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{y^{p}+\frac{1}{y^{q}+1}}[/math]
 [math][\because \mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r}=0 \therefore \mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r}=-\mathrm{p}][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{y^{r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{y^{q}}{y^{p+q}+y^{q}+1} \\=\frac{y^{r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{y^{q}}{y^{r}+y^{q}+1} \\=\frac{y^{r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{y^{q}}{\frac{1}{y^{r}}+y^{q}+1} \\=\frac{y^{r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{1}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}+\frac{y^{q} y^{r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{y^{r}+1+y^{q+r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}=\frac{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}{1+y^{r}+y^{q+r}}=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad A=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\log _{e}(3+x)=2 \log _{e} x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{বা, } \log _{e}(3+x)=\log _{e} x^{2}\\\Rightarrow 3+x=x^{2}\\\Rightarrow x^{2}-\mathrm{x}-3=0\\\Rightarrow x^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{4}=3+\frac{1}{4}\\\Rightarrow \left(x-\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}=\frac{13}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x-\frac{1}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{13}}{2}[/math]
 [ঋণাত্মক সংখ্যার লগারিদম অসংজ্ঞায়িত][math]\Rightarrow x=\frac{\sqrt{13}}{2}+\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x=\frac{\sqrt{13}+1}{2}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #19 (ID: 706242)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=2\log_kx-\log_k(3+x),B=1+\log_pqr,C=1+\log_qrp[/math] এবং [math]D=1+\log_rpq.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]C=3[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{p}{q}=\frac{q}{r}.[/math]
খ. [math]A=0[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]x=\frac{1}{2}(1+\sqrt{13}).[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{B}^{-1}+\mathrm{C}^{-1}+\mathrm{D}^{-1}=1.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]C=3[/math]
 হলে, [math]1+\log _{q} r p=3[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \quad \log _{q} r p=2\\\Rightarrow r p=q^{2}\\\Rightarrow \quad r p=q . q\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \frac{p}{q}=\frac{q}{r}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]A=0[/math]
 হলে, [math]2 \log _{k} x-\log _{k}(3+x)=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \log _{k} x^{2}-\log _{k}(3+x)=0 \\\Rightarrow \log _{k} \frac{x^{2}}{3+x}=0 \\\Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}}{3+x}=k^{0}=1 \\\Rightarrow x^{2}=3+x \\\Rightarrow x^{2}-x-3=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x=\frac{-(-1) \pm \sqrt{(-1)^{2}-4.1(-3)}}{2.1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1 \pm \sqrt{1+12}}{2} \\=\frac{1}{2}(1 \pm \sqrt{13})\end{array}[/math]
যেহেতু ঋণাত্মক সংখ্যার লগারিদম সংজ্ঞায়িত নয়।[math]\therefore \quad x=\frac{1}{2}(1+\sqrt{13})[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=1+\log _{p} q r[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \quad B=\log _{p} p+\log _{p} q r\\\Rightarrow B=\log _{p} p q r\\\Rightarrow p^{B}=p q r\\\Rightarrow p=(p q r) \frac{1}{B} \ldots \ldots \text{ (i)}\end{array}[/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, [math]q=(\text { pqr })^{\frac{1}{C}} \ldots \text { ..(ii) }[/math]
এবং [math]r=(p q r)^{\frac{1}{D}} \ldots \ldots \text { (iii) }[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) } \times \text { (ii) } \times \text { (iii) }[/math]
 থেকে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\text { pqr }=(\mathrm{pqr})^{\frac{1}{B}} \cdot(\mathrm{pqr})^{\frac{1}{C}} \cdot(\mathrm{pqr})^{\frac{1}{D}} \\\Rightarrow (\mathrm{pqr})^{1}=(p q r) \frac{1}{B}+\frac{1}{C}+\frac{1}{D} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{B}+\frac{1}{C}+\frac{1}{D}=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore B^{-1}+C^{-1}+D^{-1}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #20 (ID: 706243)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=36 y^{2}-8 y-5, B=2 a^{3}+3 a^{2}-32 a+15[/math] এবং [math]C=\log _{4}\left(14+\sqrt{x^{2}-12 x+36}\right).[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{A}=0[/math] হলে সমীকরণটির নিশ্চায়ক নির্ণয় কর।
খ. উৎপাদক ও উপপাদ্যের সাহায্যে [math]\mathrm{B}[/math] কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{C}=2[/math] হলে, [math]x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কA = 0 হলে,[math]36 y^{2}-8 y-5=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নিশ্চায়ক [math]=(-8)^{2}-4.36(-5)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=64+720 \\=784 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=2 a^{3}+3 a^{2}-32 a+15[/math]
ধরি, [math]f(a)=2 a^{3}+3 a^{2}-32 a+15[/math]
 [math]f(-5)=2(-5)^{3}+3(-5)^{2}-32(-5)+15=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad(a+5), f(a)[/math]
 এর একটি উৎপাদক।প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=2 a^{3}+3 a^{2}-32 a+15[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2 a^{3}+10 a^{2}-7 a^{2}-35 a+3 a+15 \\=2 a^{2}(a+5)-7 a(a+5)+3(a+5) \\=(a+5)\left(2 a^{2}-7 a+3\right) \\=(a+5)\left(2 a^{2}-6 a-a+3\right) \\=(a+5)\{2 a(a-3)-1(a-3)\} \\=(a+5)(a-3)(2 a-1)(\text { Ans. })\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]C-2[/math]
 হলে, [math]2=\log _{4}\left(14+\sqrt{x^{2}-12 x+36}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4^{2}=14+\sqrt{x^{2}-12 x+36}\\\Rightarrow 16-14=\sqrt{x^{2}-12 x+36}\\\Rightarrow 2=\sqrt{x^{2}-12 x+36}\\\Rightarrow 4=x^{2}-12 x+36\\\Rightarrow x^{2}-12 x+32=0\\\Rightarrow x^{2}-8 x-4 x+32=0\\\Rightarrow x(x-8)-4(x-8)=0\\\Rightarrow (x-8)(x-4)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]x-8=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x=8[/math]
অথবা, [math]x-4=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x=4[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x=4,8 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #21 (ID: 706244)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: All Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p=1+\log _{a}(b c), q=1+\log _{b}(c a), r=1+\log _{c}(a b)[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=7 x y[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]p^{-1}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{q}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{r}}=1.[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\log \left(\frac{x+y}{3}\right)=\frac{1}{2}(\log x+\log y)[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]p=1+\log _{a} b c[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{বা, } p=\log _{a} a+\log _{a} b c\\\Rightarrow p=\log _{a} a b c\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}=\frac{1}{\log _{a} a b c}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad p^{-1}=\log _{a b c} a\left[\because \log _{b} a \times \log _{a} b=1\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]p=1+\log _{a} b c[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow p=\log _{a} a+\log _{a} b c\\\Rightarrow p=\log _{a} a b c\\\Rightarrow a^{p}=a b c\\\Rightarrow a=(a b c) \frac{1}{p} \ldots \ldots \text{ (i)}\end{array}[/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, [math]b=(a b c)^{\frac{1}{q}}....\text { (ii) }[/math]
এবং [math]c=(a b c)^{\frac{1}{r}} \ldots \ldots \text { (iii) }[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) } \times \text { (ii) } \times \text { (iii) }[/math]
 থেকে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}a b c=(a b c) \frac{1}{p} \cdot(a b c) \frac{1}{\mathrm{q}} \cdot(\mathrm{abc})^{\frac{1}{r}} \\\Rightarrow (a b c)^{1}=(a b c) \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{q}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{r}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}a b c=(a b c) \frac{1}{p} \cdot(a b c) \frac{1}{\mathrm{q}} \cdot(\mathrm{abc})^{\frac{1}{r}} \\\Rightarrow (a b c)^{1}=(a b c) \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{q}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{r}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{q}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{r}}=1[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=7 x y[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}+2 x y=7 x y+2 x y[/math]
 [উভয় পক্ষে 2xy যোগ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (x+y)^{2}=9 x y\\\Rightarrow \frac{(x+y)^{2}}{9}=x y\\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{x+y}{3}\right)^{2} = x y\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log \left(\frac{x+y}{3}\right)^{2}=\log (x y)[/math]
 [উভয় পক্ষে log.নিয়ে][math]\Rightarrow 2 \log \left(\frac{x+y}{3}\right)=\log (x y)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log \left(\frac{x+y}{3}\right)=\frac{1}{2} \log (x y)=\frac{1}{2}(\log x+\log y)[/math]
 [math][\because \log (M \times N)=\log M+\log N][/math]
 [math]\therefore \log \left(\frac{x+y}{3}\right)=\frac{1}{2}(\log x+\log y)[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #22 (ID: 706245)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=x^{a-b}, Q=x^{b-c}, R=x^{c-a}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\log \left(\frac{\mathrm{P}}{\mathrm{R}}\right)=0[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]b+c=2 a.[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{1+Q+P^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+R+Q^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+P+R^{-1}}=1[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](c+a) \log (P Q)+(a+b) \log (Q R)+(b+c) \log (P R)=0[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=x^{a-b}, Q=x^{b-c}, R=x^{c-a}[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]\log \left(\frac{P}{R}\right)=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \log \left(\frac{x^{a-b}}{x^{c-a}}\right)=0\\\Rightarrow \log x^{a-b-c+a}=\log 1[\because \log 1=0]\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{x}^{2 \mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}-\mathrm{c}}=1\\\Rightarrow \quad x^{2 a-b-c}=x^{0}\left[\because x^{0}=1\right]\\\Rightarrow 2 a-b-c=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad b+c=2 a[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খবামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1}{1+Q+P^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+R+Q^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+P+R^{-1}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{1+x^{b-c}+\left(x^{a-b}\right)^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+x^{c-a}+\left(x^{b-c}\right)^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+x^{a-b}+\left(x^{c-a}\right)^{-1}}[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{x^{-b}}{x^{-b}\left(1+x^{b-c}+x^{b-a}\right)}+\frac{x^{-c}}{x^{-c}\left(1+x^{c-a}+x^{c-b}\right)}+\frac{x^{-a}}{x^{-a}\left(1+x^{a-b}+x^{a-c}\right)} \\=\frac{x^{-b}}{x^{-b}+x^{-c}+x^{-a}}+\frac{x^{-c}}{x^{-c}+x^{-a}+x^{-b}}+\frac{x^{-a}}{x^{-a}+x^{-b}+x^{-c}} \\=\frac{x^{-b}+x^{-c}+x^{-a}}{x^{-a}+x^{-b}+x^{-c}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=1=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1}{1+Q+P^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+R+Q^{-1}}+\frac{1}{1+P+R^{-1}}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) ) [math]\\[/math]
 গবামপক্ষ [math]=(c+a) \log (\mathrm{PQ})+(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}) \log (\mathrm{QR})+(\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}) \log (\mathrm{PR})[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}=(c+a) \log \left(x^{a-b} \cdot x^{b-c}\right)+(a+b) & \log \left(x^{b-c} \cdot x^{c-a}\right) \\& +(b+c)) \log \left(x^{a-b} \cdot x^{c-a}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}=(c+a) \log \left(x^{a-b+b-c}\right)+(a+b) & \log \left(x^{b-c+c-a}\right) \\& +(b+c) \log \left(x^{a-b+c-a}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\log x^{(a-c)(a+c)}+\log x^{(b-a)(b+a)}+\log x^{(c-b)(c+b)} \\=\log \left(x^{a^{2}-c^{2}} \cdot x^{b^{2}-a^{2}} \cdot x^{c^{2}-b^{2}}\right) \\=\log \left(x^{a^{2}-c^{2}+b^{2}-a^{2}+c^{2}-b^{2}}\right) \\=\log x^{0} \\=\log 1\left[\because x^{0}=1\right] \\=0[\because \log 1=0]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore(c+a) \log (P Q)+(a+b) \log (Q R)+(b+c) \log (P R)=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #23 (ID: 706246)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a=\log _{p}(q r), b=\log _{q}(r p), c=\log _{r}(p q)[/math] এবং [math]F(x)=x^{3}+6 x^{2}+11 x+6.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]c=2[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]r=\sqrt{\mathrm{pq}}.[/math]
খ. [math]F(x)[/math] কে [math]x-u[/math] এবং [math]x-v[/math] দ্বারা ভাগ করলে একই ভাগশেষ থাকে যেখানে, [math]\mathbf{u} \neq \mathbf{v},[/math] তবে দেখাও যে, [math]u^{2}+v^{2}+u v+6 u+6 v+11=0.[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{a+1}+\frac{1}{b+1}+\frac{1}{c+1}=1.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]c=\log _{\mathrm{r}}(p q)[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]c=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{\mathrm{r}}(\mathrm{pq})=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow r^{2}=p q[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \log _{8} x=y\right.[/math]
 হলে, [math]\left.a^{y}=x\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad r=\sqrt{p q}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]F(x)=x^{3}+6 x^{2}+11 x+6[/math]
এখন, [math]\mathrm{F}(\mathrm{x})[/math]
 কে [math](x-u)[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করলে ভাগশেষ হবে[math]F(u)=u^{3}+6 u^{2}+11 u+6[/math]
এবং [math](x-v)[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করলে ভাগশেষ হবে[math]F(v)=v^{3}+6 v^{2}+11 v+6[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]F(u)=F(v)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow u^{3}+6 u^{2}+11 u+6 \doteq v^{3}+6 v^{2}+11 v+6\\\Rightarrow u^{3}-v^{3}+6 u^{2}-6 v^{2}+11 u-11 v=0\\\Rightarrow (u-v)\left(u^{2}+u v+v^{2}\right)+6(u+v)(u-v)+11(u-v)=0\\\Rightarrow (u-v)\left(u^{2}+u v+v^{2}+6 u+6 v+11\right)=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad u^{2}+v^{2}+u v+6 u+6 v+11=0[/math]
 [math][\because u 
eq v[/math]
 তাই [math]u-v 
eq 0][/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]a=\log _{p}(q r), b=\log _{q}(r p)[/math]
 এবং [math]c=\log _{r}(p q)[/math]
এখন, [math]a+1=\log _{p}(q r)+1=\log _{p}(q r)+\log _{p} p=\log _{p}(p q r)[/math]
একইভাবে,[math]\begin{array}{l}b+1=\log _{q}(\text { pqr }) \\c+1=\log _{r}(\text { pqr })\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1}{a+1}+\frac{1}{b+1}+\frac{1}{c+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\log _{p}(\mathrm{pqr})}+\frac{1}{\log _{q}(\mathrm{pqr})}+\frac{1}{\log _{r}(\mathrm{pqr})}[/math]
 [math]=\log _{(\mathrm{pqr})} p+\log _{(\mathrm{pqr})} q+\log _{(\mathrm{pqr})} \mathrm{r}=\log _{(\mathrm{pqr})}(\mathrm{pqr})=1[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \frac{1}{a+1}+\frac{1}{b+1}+\frac{1}{c+1}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question:
[math]p^{2}+2=\sqrt[3]{49}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{49}} p \geq 0[/math] এবং [math]Q(x)=2^{1-x}[/math] যেখানে [math]- 4≤x≤4.[/math]
ক) [math]F(x)=\frac{x-3}{|x-3|}[/math] এর রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।
খ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]7 p^{3}+21 p=48[/math]
গ) [math]Q(x)[/math] ফাংশনটির লেখচিত্র হতে রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]F(x)=\frac{x-3}{|x-3|}[/math]
 [math]F(x)[/math]
 এর হরে সম্ভাব্য রাশি দুটি [math]x-3[/math]
 এবং [math](x-3)[/math]
 ।হরের রাশিটি [math]x-3[/math]
 হলে [math]F(x)=\frac{x-3}{x-3}=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় রেঞ্জ [math]\mathbf{R}_{\mathrm{F}}=\{-1,1\} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]p^{2}+2=\sqrt[3]{49}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{49}}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{2}=49^{\frac{1}{3}}+49^{-\frac{1}{3}}-2.1[/math]
 বা, [math]p^{2}=7^{\frac{2}{3}}+7^{-\frac{2}{3}}-2.7^{0}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{2}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot 7^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 7^{-\frac{1}{3}}+\left(7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{2}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2} \therefore p=7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
বা, আবার [math]p^{3}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে ঘন করে।]বা, [math]p^{3}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3.7^{\frac{1}{3}} .7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]p^{3}=7-\frac{1}{7}-3.1 . p[/math]
 বা [math]7 p^{3}=49-1-21 p[/math]
বা, [math]\therefore 7 p^{3}+21 p=48[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]Q(x)=2^{1-x} a[/math]
 যেখানে [math]4≤x≤4[/math]
 [math]x[/math]
 এর বিভিন্ন মানের জন্য [math]Q(x)[/math]
 এর মান নির্ণয় করি এবং অনুরূপ বিন্দুগুলো গ্রাফ পেপারে স্থাপন করে [math]Q(x)=2^{1-x}[/math]
 এর লেখ অঙ্কন করি।[math]\begin{array}{|c|c|c|c|c|c|c|c|}\hline \mathrm{x} & -4 & -2 & -1 & 0 & 1 & 2 & 4 \\\hline \mathrm{Q}(\mathrm{x}) & 32 & 8 & 4 & 2 & 1 & 0.5 & 0.125 \\\hline\end{array}[/math]

[Image]
গ্রাফ হতে দেখা যায় [math]-4≤x≤4[/math]
 সীমার মধ্যে [math]Q(x)[/math]
 এর প্রান্তিক মানদ্বয় [math]32[/math]
 ও [math]0.125[/math]
 [math]Q(-4)=2^{1-(-4)}=2^{5}=32[/math]
 এবং [math]Q(4)=2^{1-4}=2^{-3}=0.125[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত সীমার মধ্যে রেঞ্জ [math]=0.125 \leq Q(x) \leq 32[/math]
 [math]=[0.125, 32] (Ans.)[/math]

ক) [math]25^{\mathrm{a}}=125^{\mathrm{b}}[/math] হলে [math]\frac{3 a}{2 b}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ) [math]D=0[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]p^{3}-9 p^{2}+12 p=12[/math]
গ) [math]C = 2[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]y=\frac{\sqrt{21}+1}{2}[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer:

 বা, [math]5^{2 \mathrm{a}}=5^{3 \mathrm{~b}}[/math]
বা, [math]2a = 36[/math]
 বা, [math]\frac{a}{b}=\frac{3}{2}[/math]
 বা, [math]\frac{3 a}{2 b}=\frac{3 \times 3}{2 \times 2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{3 a}{2 b}=\frac{9}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]

 [উভয়পক্ষকে ঘন করে।বা, [math]p^{3}-3 . p^{2} 3+3 . p .3^{2}-3^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{2}{3}}\right)^{3}+\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}+3.5^{\frac{2}{3}} 5^{\frac{1}{3}}\left(5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]

বা, [math]p^{3}-9 p^{2}+27 p-57-15 p+45=0[/math]

 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]

Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \mathrm{r}^{2}+\sqrt[3]{8}=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{-\frac{2}{3}}[/math] [math]\text { (ii) } \mathrm{a}=5+\log _{x}(\mathrm{yz}), \mathrm{b}=7+\log _{y}(\mathrm{zx}), \mathrm{c}=9+\log _{z}(\mathrm{xy}) \text {. }[/math]
ক) [math]\log _{\sqrt{27}} \mathrm{~m}=2 \frac{2}{3}[/math] হয়, তবে [math]m[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ) (i) নং হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]5 r^{3}+15 r-24=0[/math]
গ) (ii) নং হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](a-4)^{-1}+(b-6)^{-1}+(c-8)^{-1}=1 \text {. }[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\log _{\sqrt{27}} m=\frac{8}{3}[/math]
 বা, [math]m=(\sqrt{27})^{\frac{8}{3}}=\left(3^{\frac{3}{2}}\right)^{\frac{8}{3}}=3^{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{m}=81 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\mathrm{r}^{2}+\sqrt[3]{8}=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]r^{2}+\left(2^{3}\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]
 বা, [math]r^{2}+2=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]r^{2}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot 5^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 5^{\frac{-1}{3}}+\left(5^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]r^{2}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\left.r=5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}} \right\rvert\,[/math]
 [বর্গমূল করে]...... (i)বা, [math]r^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [ঘন করে]বা, [math]r^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(5^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot 5^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}-5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]r^{3}=5-5^{-1}-3.5^{0} \cdot r \cdot[(i)[/math]
 [(i) থেকে মান বসিয়ে]বা, [math]r^{3}=5-\frac{1}{5}-3 r[/math]
 বা, [math]r^{3}=\frac{25-1-15 r}{5}[/math]
বা, [math]5 r^{3}=24-15 r[/math]
 [math]\therefore 5 r^{3}+15 r-24=0[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]a=5+\log _{x} y z[/math]
বা, [math]a-4=5+\log _{x} y z-4[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষে (-4) যোগ করে]বা, [math]a-4=1+\log _{x} y z[/math]
বা, [math]a-4=\log _{x} x+\log _{x} y z\left[\because \log _{x} x=1\right][/math]
বা, [math]a-4=\log _{x} x y z[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{1}{a-4}=\frac{1}{\log _{x} x y z}[/math]
 [বিপরীতকরণ করে]বা, [math](a-4)^{-1}=\log _{x y z} x \ldots \ldots \ldots(i)[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm{b}=7+\log _{\mathrm{y}} \mathrm{zx}[/math]
 হতে অনুরূপভাবে পাই,[math](b-6)^{-1}=\log _{x y z} y \ldots \ldots .[/math]
সমীকরণ [math](i), (ii)[/math]
 ও [math](iii)[/math]
 যোগ করে পাই,[math](a-4)^{-1}+(b-6)^{-1}+(c-8)^{-1}[/math]
 [math]=\log _{x y z} x+\log _{x y z} y+\log _{x y z} z[/math]
 [math]=\log _{x y z} x y z=1\left[\because \log _{a} a=1\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore(a-4)^{-1}+(b-6)^{-1}+(c-8)^{-1}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #27 (ID: 706235)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: CB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{-\frac{2}{3}}[/math] এবং [math]a^{2}+b^{2}=18 a b .[/math]
ক) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^{\log _{a} y}=y^{\log _{a} x}[/math]
খ) [math]P = a² + 2[/math] এবং [math]a ≥ 0[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]a^{3}+3 a=\frac{8}{3}[/math]
গ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\log _{k}\left(\frac{a-b}{4}\right)=\log _{k} \sqrt{a}+\log _{k} \sqrt{b} .[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, [math]A=x^{\log _{a} y}[/math]
বা, [math]\log _{a} A=\log _{a} x^{\log _{a} y}[/math]
 [math]=\log _{a} y \cdot \log _{a} x \ldots \ldots \ldots \ldots \ldots . . . .(i)[/math]
এবং [math]B=y \log _{a} x[/math]
বা, [math]\log _{a} B=\log _{a} y^{\log _{a} x}[/math]
 [math]=\log _{a} x \cdot \log _{a} y \ldots \ldots . . . . . \text { (ii) }[/math]
 [math](i)[/math]
 ও [math](ii)[/math]
 হতে পাই, [math]\log _{\mathrm{a}} A=\log _{\mathrm{a}} \mathrm{B}[/math]
 B, বা, [math]A = B[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathbf{x}^{\log _{a} y}=\mathbf{y}^{\log _{a} x}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathbf{P}=\mathrm{a}^{2}+2[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm{P}=3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]
 [উদ্দীপক হতে পাই।][math]\therefore \mathrm{a}^{2}+2=3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}=3^{\frac{2}{3}}-2+3^{\frac{-2}{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 3^{\frac{-1}{3}}+\left(3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [বর্গমূল করে]বা, [math]a^{3}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [ঘন করে]বা, [math]a^{3}=\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]a^{3}=3-3^{-1}-3.3^{\frac{1}{3}-\frac{1}{3}} \cdot a\left[\because 3^{\frac{1}{3}}-3^{\frac{-1}{3}}=a\right][/math]
বা, [math]a^{3}=3-\frac{1}{3}-3 \cdot 3^{0} \cdot a \quad[/math]
 বা, [math]a^{3}=3-\frac{1}{3}-3 a \quad\left[\because 3^{0}=1\right][/math]
বা, [math]a^{3}=\frac{9-1-9 a}{3}[/math]
 বা, [math]3 a^{3}=8-9 a[/math]
 বা, [math]3\left(a^{3}+3 a\right)=8[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}^{3}+3 \mathrm{a}=\frac{8}{3}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]a^{2}+b^{2}=18 a b[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}-2 a b+b^{2}=16 a b[/math]
 বা, [math](a-b)^{2}=16 a b[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(a-b)^{2}}{16}=a b[/math]
 বা, [math]\frac{a-b}{4}=\sqrt{a b}[/math]
 [বর্গমূল করে][math]\log _{k}\left(\frac{a-b}{4}\right)=\log _{k}(\sqrt{a b})[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষে [math]log_x[/math]
 নিয়ে][math]\therefore \log _{k}\left(\frac{a-b}{4}\right)=\log _{k} \sqrt{a}+\log _{k} \sqrt{b}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #28 (ID: 706124)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p^{2}+2=\sqrt[3]{49}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{49}}, p \geq 0[/math] এবং [math]f(x)=\ln \frac{6+x}{6-x}[/math]
ক) [math]\sqrt{y^{2} \sqrt{y^{6} \sqrt{y^{4}}}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ) প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]7 p^{3}+21 p=48[/math]
গ) f(x) এর ডোমেন ও রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\sqrt{y^{2} \sqrt{y^{6} \sqrt{y^{4}}}}=\sqrt{y^{8} \sqrt{y^{6} \cdot y^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{y^{8} \cdot \sqrt{y^{8}}}=\sqrt{y^{8} \cdot y^{4}}=\sqrt{y^{12}}=y^{6} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]p^{2}+2=\sqrt[3]{49}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{49}}[/math]
 বা, [math]p^{2}+2=\sqrt[3]{7^{2}}+\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{7^{2}}}[/math]
বা, [math]\mathrm{p}^{2}=7^{\frac{2}{3}}+7^{-\frac{2}{3}}-2[/math]
 বা, [math]\mathrm{p}^{2}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot 7^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 7^{-\frac{1}{3}}+\left(7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{2}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{2}[/math]
 বা, [math]p=7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{3}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{3}=\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3.7^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 7^{-\frac{1}{3}} \cdot\left(7^{\frac{1}{3}}-7^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]\mathrm{p}^{3}=7-7^{-1}-3.7^{\frac{1}{3}-\frac{1}{3}} \cdot \mathrm{p}[/math]
বা, [math]p^{3}=7-\frac{1}{7}-3 p[/math]
বা, [math]7 p^{3}=49-1-21 p[/math]
 [math]\therefore 7 p^{3}+21 p=48[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\ln \frac{6+x}{6-x}[/math]
যেহেতু লগারিদমিক ফাংশন শুধুমাত্র ধনাত্মক বাস্তব সংখ্যার জন্য সংজ্ঞায়িত হয়।[math]\therefore \frac{6+\mathrm{x}}{6-\mathrm{x}}>0[/math]
 যদি (i) } [math]6+\mathrm{x}>0[/math]
 এবং [math]6-\mathrm{x}>0[/math]
 হয়অথবা [math](ii) 6+x-6[/math]
 এবং [math]-x>-6[/math]
অর্থাৎ, [math]x > -6[/math]
 এবং [math]x  6[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]=\{x: x6\}=\varnothing[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত ফাংশনের ডোমেন[math]D_f[/math]
 = (i) ও (ii) এ প্রাপ্ত ডোমেনের সংযোগ [math]=(-6,6) \cup \varnothing=(-6,6)[/math]
ধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\ln \frac{6+x}{6-x}[/math]
 বা, [math]e^{y}=\frac{6+x}{6-x}[/math]
বা, [math]6+x=6 e^{y}-x e^{y}[/math]
 বা, [math]x\left(1+e^{y}\right)=6\left(e^{y}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]y[/math]
 এর সকল বাস্তব মানের জন্য x এর মান বাস্তব হয়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত ফাংশেনের রেঞ্জ [math]R_f=R[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]D_f=R[/math]
 = (-6, 6) এবং রেঞ্জ [math]R_f=R[/math]
 (Ans.)

Question:
[math]x-3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}-1=0[/math] এবং [math]y=\frac{3-x}{4+x}[/math]
ক) [math]1+\frac{1}{3}+\frac{1}{3^{2}}+\frac{1}{3^{3}}+[/math] ... ... .... ধারাটির অসীমতক সমষ্টি নির্ণয় কর।
খ) দেখাও যে, [math]x^{3}-3 x^{2}+12 x-16=0[/math]
গ) [math]In y = 1[/math] হলে, [math]x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কগুণোত্তর ধারাটির ১ম পদ, [math]a = 1[/math]
এবং সাধারণ অনুপাত, [math]r=\frac{1}{3}খদেওয়া আছে, [math]x-3^{\frac{2}{3}}+3^{\frac{1}{3}}-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]x-1=3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
বা, [math](x-1)^{3}=\left(3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [ঘন করে]বা, [math]x^{3}-3 x^{2}+3 x-1=\left(3^{\frac{2}{3}}\right)^{3}-\left(3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot 3^{\frac{2}{3}} \cdot 3^{\frac{1}{3}}\left(3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]
বা, [math]x^{3}-3 x^{2}+3 x-1=9-3-3.3^{\frac{2}{3}+\frac{1}{3}}(x-1)\left[\because x-1=3^{\frac{2}{3}}-3^{3}\right][/math]
বা, [math]x^{3}-3 x^{2}+3 x-1=9-3-3 \cdot 3(x-1)[/math]
বা, [math]x^{3}-3 x^{2}+3 x-1-6+9 x-9=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{3}-3 x^{2}+12 x-16=0[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]y=\frac{3-x}{4+x}[/math]
এবং [math]In y = 1.[/math]
বা, [math]y = e[/math]
 বা, [math]\frac{3-x}{4+x}=e[/math]
বা, [math]3-x=4e+ ex[/math]
 বা, [math]ex + x = 3-4e[/math]
বা, [math]x(e+1)=3-4e[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{x}=\frac{3-4 \mathrm{e}}{\mathrm{e}+1} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #30 (ID: 706126)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: BB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } m=\frac{1}{2}\{\sqrt[3]{x+y}-\sqrt[3]{x-y}\}[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}-y^{2}=z^{3}[/math] [math]\text { (ii) } n=\log (3+5 x)-2 \log x[/math]
ক) [math]a^{2}+b^{2}=11 a b[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\log \left(\frac{a-b}{3}\right)=\frac{1}{2}(\log a+\log b)[/math]
খ) [math]n = 0[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]2 x-5=\sqrt{37}[/math]
গ) (i) নং হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]4 m^{3}+3 m z-y=0[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]a^{2}+b^{2}=11 a b[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}+b^{2}-2 a b=11 a b-2 a b[/math]
বা, [math](a-b)^{2}=9 a b[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{(a-b)^{2}}{9}=a b[/math]
 [9 দ্বারা ভাগ করে]বা, [math]\left(\frac{a-b}{3}\right)^{2}=a b[/math]
বা, [math]\log \left(\frac{a-b}{3}\right)^{2}=\log a b[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষে log নিয়ে][math]\therefore 2 \log \frac{a-b}{3}=\log a b[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log \left(\frac{a-b}{3}\right)=\frac{1}{2}(\log a+\log b)[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত),[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]n = log(3+5x)-2logx[/math]
এবং [math]n = 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log (3+5 x)-2 \log x=0[/math]
বা, [math]\log (3+5 x)-\log x^{2}=0[/math]
বা, [math]\log \left(\frac{3+5 x}{x^{2}}\right)=\log (1)[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{3+5 x}{x^{2}}=1[/math]
 বা, [math]x^{2}-5 x-3=0 \text {. }[/math]
বা, [math]x=\frac{-(-5) \pm \sqrt{(-5)^{2}-4 \cdot 1 \cdot(-3)}}{2 \cdot 1}[/math]
বা, [math]x=\frac{5 \pm \sqrt{25+12}}{2}=\frac{5 \pm \sqrt{37}}{2}[/math]
বা, [math]2 x=5 \pm \sqrt{37}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 x-5= \pm \sqrt{37}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 x-5=\sqrt{37}[/math]
 [ঋণাত্মক সংখ্যার লগারিদম অগ্রহণযোগ্য][math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]m=\frac{1}{2}(\sqrt[3]{x+y}-\sqrt[3]{x-y})[/math]
 এবং [math]x^{2}-y^{2}=z^{3}[/math]
এখন, [math]m=\frac{1}{2}(\sqrt[3]{x+y}-\sqrt[3]{x-y})[/math]
বা, [math]2 m=\sqrt[3]{x+y}-\sqrt[3]{x-y}[/math]
বা, [math]8 m^{3}=\left\{(x+y)^{\frac{1}{3}}\right\}^{3}-\left\{(x-y)^{\frac{1}{3}}\right\}^{3}-3(x+y)^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot(x-y)^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
 [math]\left\{(x+y)^{\frac{1}{3}}-(x-y)^{\frac{1}{3}}\right\}[/math]
 [ঘন করে][math]\begin{array}{l} 8 m^{3}=(x+y-x+y)-3\left(x^{2}-y^{2}\right)^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 2 m \\\cdot\left[\because(x+y)^{\frac{1}{3}}-(x-y)^{\frac{1}{3}}=2 m\right]\end{array}[/math]
বা, [math]8 m^{3}=2 y-3\left(z^{3}\right)^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 2 m[/math]
বা, [math]4 m^{3}=y-3 m z[/math]
বা, [math]\therefore 4 m^{3}+3 m z-y=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #31 (ID: 706127)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]M=\frac{1}{a^{y}+a^{-z}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{z}+a^{-x}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{x}+a^{-y}+1}[/math] এবং [math]A=4^{x}-3.2^{x+2}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]a^{a \sqrt{a}}=(a \sqrt{a})^{a}[/math] হলে, [math]a[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]x + y + z = 0[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]M = 1[/math]
গ. [math]A = - 32[/math] হলে, [math]x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]a^{a \sqrt{a}}=(a \sqrt{a})^{a} \Rightarrow \left(a^{a \sqrt{a}}\right)^{\frac{1}{a}}=\left\{(a \sqrt{a})^{a}\right\}^{\frac{1}{a}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a^{\sqrt{a}}=a \sqrt{a} \Rightarrow a^{\sqrt{a}}=a^{1} \cdot a^{\frac{1}{2}} \\\Rightarrow a^{\sqrt{a}}=a^{1+\frac{1}{2}} \Rightarrow a^{\sqrt{a}}=a^{\frac{3}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{a}=\frac{3}{2} \therefore a=\frac{9}{4} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}M=\frac{1}{a^{y}+a^{-z}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{z}+a^{-x}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{x}+a^{-y}+1} \\=\frac{1}{a^{y}+\frac{1}{a^{z}}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{z}+a^{-x}+1}+\frac{1}{a^{x}+a^{-y}+1}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{1}{a^{x}+\frac{1}{a^{y}}+1}[/math]
 [math][\because x+y+z=0 \therefore y+z=-x][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{a^{z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{a^{y}}{a^{x+y}+a^{y}+} \\=\frac{a^{z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{a^{y}}{a^{-z}+a^{y}+1} \\=\frac{a^{z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{a^{y}}{\frac{1}{a^{z}}+a^{y}+1} \\=\frac{a^{z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{1}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}+\frac{a^{y} \cdot a^{z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}} \\=\frac{a^{z}+1+a^{y+z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}=\frac{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}{1+a^{z}+a^{y+z}}=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore M=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=4^{x}-3.2^{x+2}[/math]
 এবং [math]A=-32[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore 4^{x}-3 \cdot 2^{x+2}=-32 \\\Rightarrow \left(2^{2}\right)^{x}-3 \cdot 2^{x+2}=-32 \\\Rightarrow 2^{2 x}-3 \cdot 2^{x+2}=-32\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(2^{x}\right)^{2}-3 \cdot 2^{2} \cdot 2^{x}=-32[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \mathrm{a}^{\mathrm{mn}}=\left(\mathrm{a}^{\mathrm{m}}\right)^{\mathrm{n}}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]\left.a^{m+n}=a^{m} \cdot a^{n}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(2^{x}\right)^{2}-12.2^{x}+32=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a^{2}-12 a+32=0[/math]
 [ [math]2^{x}=a[/math]
 ধরে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{a}^{2}-8 \mathrm{a}-4 \mathrm{a}+32=0\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}-8)-4(\mathrm{a}-8)=0\\\Rightarrow (a-4)(a-8)=0\end{array}[/math]
হয়, [math]a-4=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore a=4[/math]
এখন,[math]a = 4[/math]
 হলে,[math]\begin{aligned}& 2^{x}=4 \\\Rightarrow & 2^{x}=2^{2} \\\therefore & x=2\end{aligned}[/math]
অথবা,[math]a-8=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a=8[/math]
আবার, [math]a = 8[/math]
 হলে,[math]2^{x}=8[/math]
 [মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2^{x}=2^{3} \\\therefore x=3\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math]x=2,3 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #32 (ID: 706128)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: MSB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P(x)=2 x^{3}+x^{2}-18 x-9 K[/math] এবং [math]Q(x)=\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x^{3}-x^{2}-2 x}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\log _{\sqrt{2}} 4-\log _{9} 3[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ৷
খ. [math]2 \mathrm{x}+1, \mathrm{P}(\mathrm{x})[/math] এর একটি উৎপাদক হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]K = 1[/math]
গ. [math]Q(x)[/math] কে আংশিক ভগ্নাংশে প্রকাশ কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\log _{\sqrt{2}} 4-\log _{9} 3=\log _{\sqrt{2}}(\sqrt{2})^{4}-\log _{9} 9^{\frac{1}{2}} \\=4 \log _{\sqrt{2}} \sqrt{2}-\frac{1}{2} \log _{9} 9=4.1-\frac{1}{2} .1=4-\frac{1}{2}=\frac{7}{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P(x)=2 x^{3}+x^{2}-18 x-9 K[/math]
 [math]P(x)[/math]
 এর একটি উৎপাদক [math](2x + 1)[/math]
 হলে, [math]P\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore 2 \cdot\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)^{3}+\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}-18\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right)-9 \mathrm{k}=0 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cdot\left(-\frac{1}{8}\right)+\frac{1}{4}+9-9 \mathrm{k}=0 \\\Rightarrow -\frac{1}{4}+\frac{1}{4}+9-9 \mathrm{k}=0 \Rightarrow 9-9 \mathrm{k}=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 9 k=9 \therefore k=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\begin{array}{l}Q(x)=\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x^{3}-x^{2}-2 x}=\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x\left(x^{2}-x-2\right)}=\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x\left(x^{2}-2 x+x-2\right)} \\=\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x\{x(x-2)+1(x-2)\}}=\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x(x-2)(x+1)}\end{array}[/math]
মনে করি, [math]\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x(x-2)(x+1)} \equiv \frac{A}{x}+\frac{B}{x-2}+\frac{C}{x+1} \cdots \cdots \text { (i) }[/math]
(i) নং এর উভয় পক্ষকে [math]x(x – 2 ) (x + 1)[/math]
 দ্বারা গুণ করে পাই,[math]x^{2}-3 x-2 \equiv A(x-2)(x+1)+B x(x+1)+C x(x-2) \ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }[/math]
(ii) নং-এ [math]x = 0[/math]
 বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}0-3 \cdot 0-2=\mathrm{A}(0-2)(0+1)+\mathrm{B} \cdot 0(0+1)+\mathrm{C} .0(0-2) \\\Rightarrow -2=\mathrm{A} \cdot(-2) \cdot 1+0+0 \Rightarrow -2=-2 \mathrm{~A} \quad \therefore \mathrm{A}=1\end{array}[/math]
আবার, (ii) নং এ [math]x = 2[/math]
 বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}2^{2}-3.2-2=\mathrm{A}: 0.3+\mathrm{B} .2 .3+\text { C. } 2.0 \\\Rightarrow 4-8=6 \mathrm{~B} \Rightarrow -4=6 \mathrm{~B} \quad \therefore \mathrm{B}=-\frac{2}{3}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, (ii) নং সমীকরণে [math]x = − 1[/math]
 বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}(-1)^{2}-3 \cdot(-1)-2=\mathrm{A} \cdot 0+\mathrm{B} \cdot 0+\mathrm{C} \cdot(-1)(-3) \\\Rightarrow 1+3-2=3 \mathrm{C} \Rightarrow 2=3 \mathrm{C} \therefore \mathrm{C}=\frac{2}{3}\end{array}[/math]
A, B ও C এর মান (i) নং এ বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\frac{x^{2}-3 x-2}{x(x-2)(x+1)} \equiv \frac{1}{x}+\frac{\frac{-2}{3}}{x-2}+\frac{\frac{2}{3}}{x+1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore Q(x) \equiv \frac{1}{x}-\frac{2}{3(x-2)}+\frac{2}{3(x+1)}[/math]
 ইহাই নির্ণেয় আংশিক ভগ্নাংশ [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:

Question #33 (ID: 706129)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=1+\log _{p} q r, B=2+\log _{q} r p, C=3+\log _{\mathrm{r}} p q[/math] এবং [math]m=2+2^{\frac{2}{3}}+2^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]

Options:
ক. B = 4 হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{p}{q}=\frac{q}{r}[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{\mathrm{~A}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~B}-1}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{C}-2}=1.[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]m^{3}-6 m^{2}+6 m-2=0.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=2+\log _{q} r p[/math]
 [math]B=4[/math]
 হলে, [math]2+\log _{q} r p=4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{\mathrm{q}} \mathrm{pr}=2 \Rightarrow \mathrm{q}^{2}=\mathrm{pr}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{q}{p}=\frac{r}{q}[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে pq দ্বারা ভাগ করে ][math]\therefore \frac{p}{q}=\frac{q}{r}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=1+\log _{p}(q r)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow A=\log _{\mathrm{p}} \mathrm{p}+\log _{\mathrm{p}}(\mathrm{qr}) \\\therefore A=\log _{\mathrm{p}} \text { (pqr) }\end{array}[/math]
আবার, [math]B=2+\log _{q}(r p)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow { B-1 }=1+\log _{q}(r p) \\\Rightarrow { B-1 }=\log _{q} q+\log _{q}(r p) \therefore B-1=\log _{q}(p q r)\end{array}[/math]
এবং [math]C=3+\log _{r}(p q)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-2=1+\log _{r}(\mathrm{pq}) \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}-2=\log _{\mathrm{r}} \mathrm{r}+\log _{r}(\mathrm{pq}) \therefore \mathrm{C}-2=\log _{\mathrm{r}}(\mathrm{pqr})\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{1}{A}+\frac{1}{B-1}+\frac{1}{C-2}=\frac{1}{\log _{p}(p q r)}+\frac{1}{\log _{q}(p q r)}+\frac{1}{\log _{r}(p q r)}[/math]
 [math]=\log _{\mathrm{pqr}} p+\log _{p q r} q+\log _{p q r} r=\log _{(p q r)}(p q r)=1=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1}{\mathrm{~A}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~B}-1}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{C}-2}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]m=2+2^{\frac{2}{3}}+2^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow m-2=2^{\frac{2}{3}}+2^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (m-2)^{3}=\left(2^{\frac{2}{3}}+2^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [উভয়পক্ষকে ঘন করে][math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}-3 \cdot \mathrm{m}^{2} \cdot 2+3 \mathrm{~m} \cdot 2^{2}-2^{3}=\left(2^{\frac{2}{3}}\right)^{3}+\left(2^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}+3 \cdot 2^{\frac{2}{3}} \cdot 2^{\frac{1}{3}}\left(2^{\frac{2}{3}}+2^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left[\because(x+y)^{3}=x^{3}+y^{3}+3 x y(x+y)\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \dot{m}^{3}-6 \mathrm{~m}^{2}+12 \mathrm{~m}-8=2^{2}+2+3.2^{\frac{2}{3}}+\frac{1}{3} \cdot(\mathrm{m}-2)[/math]
 [math]\left[\because 2^{\frac{2}{3}}+2^{\frac{1}{3}}=m-2\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow m^{3}-6 m^{2}+12 m-8=4+2+3 \cdot 2^{1}(m-2)\\\Rightarrow m^{3}-6 m^{2}+12 m-8=6+6 m-12\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore m^{3}-6 m^{2}+6 m-2=0[/math]
 (প্ৰমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #34 (ID: 706130)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^{2}+b^{2}=14 a b[/math] এবং [math]m^{2}-2=\sqrt[3]{5^{2}}+\sqrt[3]{5^{-2}}.[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]8^{x}=32^{y}[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{x}{y}[/math] নির্ণয় করো।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]\log \left(\frac{a+b}{4}\right)=\frac{1}{2} \log a+\frac{1}{2} \log b.[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ করো যে, [math]5 m^{3}-15 m=26[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]8^{x}=32^{y}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(2^{3}\right)^{x}=\left(2^{5}\right)^{y} \Rightarrow 2^{3 x}=2^{5 y} \Rightarrow 3 x=5 y \therefore \frac{x}{y}=\frac{5}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a^{2}+b^{2}=14 a b[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (a+b)^{2}-2 a b=14 a b\\\Rightarrow (a+b)^{2}=16 a b\\\Rightarrow \left(\frac{a+b}{4}\right)^{2}=a b\\\Rightarrow \log \left(\frac{a+b}{4}\right)^{2}=\log a b\\\Rightarrow 2 \log \left(\frac{a+b}{4}\right)=\log a+\log b\\\Rightarrow \log \left(\frac{a+b}{4}\right)=\frac{1}{2}(\log a+\log b)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log \left(\frac{a+b}{4}\right)=\frac{1}{2} \log a+\frac{1}{2} \log b[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]m^{2}-2=\sqrt[3]{5^{2}}+\sqrt[3]{5^{-2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow m^{2}=\sqrt[3]{5^{2}}+\sqrt[3]{5^{-2}}+2 \\\Rightarrow m^{2}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}+5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{2} \therefore m=5^{\frac{1}{3}}+5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]m^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}+5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right)^{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}+\left(5^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}+3.5^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}+5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right) \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=5+\frac{1}{5}+3 \mathrm{~m}\left[\because \mathrm{m}=5^{\frac{1}{3}}+5^{\frac{-1}{3}}\right] \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{m}^{3}=\frac{25+1+15 \mathrm{~m}}{5}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 5 \mathrm{~m}^{3}=26+15 \mathrm{~m} \quad \therefore 5 \mathrm{~m}^{3}-15 \mathrm{~m}=26[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #35 (ID: 706131)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: CB

Question:
[math]p=1+\log _{x}(y z), q=1+\log _{y}(z x), r=1+\log _{z}(x y)[/math] এবং [math]y=\frac{5-x}{5+x}[/math] একটি ফাংশন।

Options:
ক. ফাংশনটির ডোমেন নির্ণয় কর।
খ. ফাংশনটির বিপরীত ফাংশন নির্ণয় কর।
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}+\frac{1}{r}=1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]y=\frac{5-x}{5+x}[/math]
y সংজ্ঞায়িত হবে যদি ও কেবল যদি [math]5+x 
eq 0 \Rightarrow x 
eq-5[/math]
 হয়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]=\{\mathbf{x} \in \mathbb{R}: \mathbf{x} 
eq-5\} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\frac{5-x}{5+x} \therefore f^{-1}(y)=x[/math]
তাহলে, [math]\frac{5-x}{5+x}=y \Rightarrow 5-x=5 y+x y \Rightarrow x y+x=5-5 y[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x(y+1)=5-5 y \Rightarrow x=\frac{5-5 y}{y+1}\\\Rightarrow f^{-1}(\mathrm{y})=\frac{5-5 \mathrm{y}}{\mathrm{y}+1} \therefore f^{-1}(\mathrm{x})=\frac{5-5 \mathrm{x}}{\mathrm{x}+1} \text{ (Ans.)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]p=1+\log _{x} y z[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow p=\log _{x} x+\log _{x} y z \Rightarrow p=\log _{x} x y z[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x^{p}=x y z[/math]
 [math]x=(x y z)^{\frac{1}{\mathrm{P}}} \ldots \ldots(\mathrm{i})[/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, [math]y=(x y z)^{\frac{1}{q}} \ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }[/math]
এবং [math]z=(x y z)^{\frac{1}{r}} \ldots \ldots \text { (iii) }[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) } \times \text { (ii) } \times(\text { (iii) }[/math]
 থেকে পাই, [math]x y z=(x y z)^{\frac{1}{p}} \cdot(x y z)^{\frac{1}{q}} \cdot(x y z)^{\frac{1}{r}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (x y z)^{1}=(x y z)^{\frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}+\frac{1}{r}} \therefore \frac{1}{p}+\frac{1}{q}+\frac{1}{r}=1[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Question #36 (ID: 706132)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \sqrt[a]{p}=\sqrt[b]{q}=\sqrt[c]{r}[/math] এবং [math]q r=\frac{1}{p} ; \text { (ii) } \frac{\log _{k} a}{q-r}=\frac{\log _{k} b}{r-p}=\frac{\log _{k} c}{p-q}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]n = 3[/math] হলে, [math]\sqrt[n]{-125}=[/math] কত?
খ. (i) উদ্দীপকের আলোকে [math](a + b + c)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. (ii) উদ্দীপক ব্যবহার করে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{rp^{2}+p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}=1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]n=3[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt[n]{-125}=\sqrt[3]{(-5)^{3}}=\left\{(-5)^{3}\right\}^{\frac{1}{3}}=-5(\text { Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sqrt[a]{p}=\sqrt[b]{q}=\sqrt[c]{r}[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm{qr}=\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}} \therefore \mathrm{pqr}=1 \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
ধরি, [math]\sqrt[a]{p}=\sqrt[b]{q}=\sqrt[c]{r}=k[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]\sqrt[\mathrm{a}]{\mathrm{p}}=\mathrm{k} \Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}}}=\mathrm{k} \quad \therefore \mathrm{p}=\mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{a}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{ll}\sqrt[\mathrm{b}]{\mathrm{q}}=\mathrm{k} \Rightarrow \mathrm{q}^{\frac{1}{\mathrm{~b}}}=\mathrm{k} & \therefore \mathrm{q}=\mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{b}} \\\sqrt[c]{\mathrm{r}}=\mathrm{k} \Rightarrow \mathrm{r}^{\frac{1}{\mathrm{c}}}=\mathrm{k} & \therefore \mathrm{r}=\mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{c}}\end{array}[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{pqr}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{a}} \mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{b}} \mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{c}}=1 \Rightarrow \mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}}=\mathrm{k}^{0} \therefore \mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}=0 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গধরি, [math]\frac{\log _{k} a}{q-r}=\frac{\log _{k} b}{r-p}=\frac{\log _{k} c}{p-q}=m[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} a=m(q-r)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(q^{2}+q r+r^{2}\right) \log _{k} a=m(q-r)\left(q^{2}+q r+r^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}}=m\left(q^{3}-r^{3}\right)........\text { (i) }[/math]
আবার, [math]\log _{k} b=m(r-p)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(r^{2}+r p+p^{2}\right) \log _{k} b=m(r-p)\left(r^{2}+r p+p^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} b^{r^{2}+p^{2}+p^{2}}=m\left(r^{3}-p^{3}\right)........\text { (ii) }[/math]
এবং [math]\log _{k} c=m(p-q)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(p^{2}+p q+q^{2}\right) \log _{k} c=m(p-q)\left(p^{2}+p q+q^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} \mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{pq}+\mathrm{q}^{2}}=\mathrm{m}\left(\mathrm{p}^{3}-\mathrm{q}^{3}\right)........\text { (iii) }[/math]
এখন, (i), (ii) ও (iii) যোগ করে পাই,[math]\therefore \log _{k} a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}}+\log _{k} b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}}+\log _{k} c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=m\left(q^{3}-r^{3}\right)+m\left(r^{3}-p^{3}\right)+m\left(p^{3}-q^{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{k}\left(a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{p^{2}+p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}\right)=m\left(q^{3}-r^{3}+r^{3}-p^{3}\right.\left.+p^{3}-q^{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{k}\left(a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}\right)=0=\log _{k} 1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #37 (ID: 706133)

Question:
[math]A=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{1}{3}} ; f(x)=\ln \frac{1+x}{1-x}[/math]

ক, [math]\frac{1}{3}+\frac{1}{3^{2}}+\frac{1}{3^{3}}+\frac{1}{3^{4}}+\ldots .[/math] ধারার অসীমতক সমষ্টি নির্ণয় কর।

Options:
খ. [math]A=2 a-3[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]8 a^{3}-36 a^{2}+24 a-12=0[/math]
গ. [math]f(x)[/math] এর ডোমেন নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত ধারা, [math]\frac{1}{3}+\frac{1}{3^{2}}+\frac{1}{3^{3}}+\frac{1}{3^{4}}+\ldots \ldots \ldots[/math]
ধারাটির ১ম পদ, [math]a=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
সাধারণ অনুপাত, [math]r=\frac{\frac{1}{3^{2}}}{\frac{1}{3}}=\frac{1}{3}খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
 [math]A=2 a-3[/math]
 হলে, [math]5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{1}{3}}=2 a-3[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}=(2 \mathrm{a}-3)^{3}[/math]
 [ঘন করে][math]\Rightarrow \left(5^{\frac{2}{3}}\right)^{3}+\left(5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}+3.5^{\frac{2}{3}} \cdot 5^{\frac{1}{3}}\left(5^{\frac{2}{3}}+5^{\frac{1}{3}}\right)=(2 a)^{3}-(3)^{3}-32 \mathrm{a} 3(2 a-3)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 5^{2}+5+3.5^{\frac{2}{3}+\frac{1}{3}} \cdot(2 a-3)=8 a^{3}-27-36 a^{2}+54 a \\\Rightarrow 25+5+3.5(2 a-3)=8 a^{3}-27-36 a^{2}+54 a \\\Rightarrow 25+5+30 a-45=8 a^{3}-27-36 a^{2}+54 a \\\Rightarrow 8 a^{3}-36 a^{2}+54 a-27+15-30 a=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 8 a^{3}-36 a^{2}+24 a-12=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত) [math]\\[/math]
 গধরি, [math]y=f(x)=\ell n \frac{1+x}{1-x}[/math]
যেহেতু লগারিদম শুধুমাত্র ধনাত্মক বাস্তব সংখ্যার জন্য সংজ্ঞায়িত হয়।[math]\therefore \frac{1+x}{1-x}>0[/math]
 যদি [math]\text { (i) } 1+x>0[/math]
 এবং [math]1-x>0[/math]
 হয়অথবা, [math]\text { (ii) } 1+x-1[/math]
 এবং [math]-x>-1 \therefore x1[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]=\{x: x1\}=\varnothing[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রদত্ত ফাংশনের ডোমেন[math]D_{f}=[/math]
 (i) ও (ii) এ প্রাপ্ত ডোমেনের সংযোগ[math]=(-1,1) \cup \varnothing=(-1,1) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #38 (ID: 706134)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: DB

Question:
[math]2^{\frac{1}{x}}=3^{\frac{1}{y}}=6^{\frac{1}{z}}[/math] এবং [math]p=2^{\frac{1}{3}}-2^{-\frac{1}{3}}-3[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]4^{2 t}=2^{t+1}[/math] হলে t এর মান নির্ণয় করো।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]x + y = z.[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]2 p\left(p^{2}+9 p+30\right)+69=0.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]4^{2 t}=2^{t+1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2^{4 t}=2^{t+1} \Rightarrow 4 t=t+1 \Rightarrow 4 t-t=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \mathrm{t}=1 \quad \therefore \mathrm{t}=\frac{1}{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]2^{\frac{1}{x}}=3^{\frac{1}{y}}=6^{\frac{1}{z}}[/math]
এখন, [math]2^{\frac{1}{x}}=6^{\frac{1}{z}}[/math]
 [math]2^{\frac{1}{x}}=6^{\frac{1}{z}}[/math]
এবং [math]3^{\frac{1}{y}}=6^{\frac{1}{z}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 3=6^{\frac{y}{z}}.........\text { (ii) }[/math]
(i) ও (ii) নং সমীকরণ গুণ করে পাই,[math]2.3=6^{\frac{x}{z}} \cdot 6^{\frac{y}{2}} \Rightarrow 6=6^{\frac{x}{2}+\frac{y}{z}} \Rightarrow 6^{1}=6^{\frac{x+y}{z}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1=\frac{x+y}{z} \therefore x+y=z[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]p=2^{\frac{1}{3}}-2^{-\frac{1}{3}}-3[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow p+3=2^{\frac{1}{3}}-2^{-\frac{1}{3}} \Rightarrow (p+3)^{3}=\left(2^{\frac{1}{3}}-2^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)^{3}\\\Rightarrow p^{3}+3^{3}+3 \cdot p \cdot 3(p+3)=2-2^{-1}-3 \cdot 2^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot 2^{-\frac{1}{3}}\left(2^{\frac{1}{3}}-2^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right)\\\Rightarrow p^{3}+27+9 p^{2}+27 p=2-\frac{1}{2}-3(p+3)\left[\because p+3=2^{\frac{1}{3}}-2^{-\frac{1}{3}}\right]\\\Rightarrow p^{3}+27+9 p^{2}+27 p=\frac{3}{2}-3 p-9\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 p^{3}+54+18 p^{2}+54 p=3-6 p-18\\\Rightarrow 2 p^{3}+54+18 p^{2}+54 p-3+6 p+18=0\\\Rightarrow 2 p^{3}+18 p^{2}+60 p+69=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 p\left(p^{2}+9 p+30\right)+69=0[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #39 (ID: 706135)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\log (x-y)=\frac{1}{2}(\log 9+\log x+\log y)[/math] এবং [math]\frac{\log _{k} a}{q-r}=\frac{\log _{k} b}{r-p}=\frac{\log _{k} c}{p-q}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\log _{2} 9 \times \log _{3} 2[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=11 x y[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}=1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\log _{2} 9 \times \log _{3} 2=\log _{2} 3^{2} \times \log _{3} 2[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2 \times \log _{2} 3 \times \log _{3} 2=2 \times \log _{2} 2\left[\because \log _{a} b \times \log _{b} a=\log _{a} a\right] \\=2 \times 1=2 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\log (x-y)=\frac{1}{2}(\log 9+\log x+\log y)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \log (x-y)=\log (9 x y) \Rightarrow \log (x-y)^{2}=\log (9 x y)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (x-y)^{2}=9 x y \Rightarrow x^{2}-2 x y+y^{2}=9 x y[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x^{2}+y^{2}=9 x y+2 x y \quad \therefore x^{2}+y^{2}=11 x y[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো) [math]\\[/math]
 গধরি, [math]\frac{\log _{k} a}{q-r}=\frac{\log _{k} b}{r-p}=\frac{\log _{k} c}{p-q}=m[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} a=m(q-r)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(q^{2}+q r+r^{2}\right) \log _{k} a=m(q-r)\left(q^{2}+q r+r^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}}=m\left(q^{3}-r^{3}\right)........\text { (i) }[/math]
আবার, [math]\log _{k} b=m(r-p)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(r^{2}+r p+p^{2}\right) \log _{k} b=m(r-p)\left(r^{2}+r p+p^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} b^{r^{2}+p^{2}+p^{2}}=m\left(r^{3}-p^{3}\right)........\text { (ii) }[/math]
এবং [math]\log _{k} c=m(p-q)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(p^{2}+p q+q^{2}\right) \log _{k} c=m(p-q)\left(p^{2}+p q+q^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \log _{k} \mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{pq}+\mathrm{q}^{2}}=\mathrm{m}\left(\mathrm{p}^{3}-\mathrm{q}^{3}\right)........\text { (iii) }[/math]
এখন, (i), (ii) ও (iii) যোগ করে পাই,[math]\therefore \log _{k} a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}}+\log _{k} b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}}+\log _{k} c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=m\left(q^{3}-r^{3}\right)+m\left(r^{3}-p^{3}\right)+m\left(p^{3}-q^{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{k}\left(a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{p^{2}+p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}\right)=m\left(q^{3}-r^{3}+r^{3}-p^{3}\right.\left.+p^{3}-q^{3}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \log _{k}\left(a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}\right)=0=\log _{k} 1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a^{q^{2}+q r+r^{2}} \cdot b^{r^{2}+r p+p^{2}} \cdot c^{p^{2}+p q+q^{2}}=1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
